Carrier haulage real time visibility product - 
Ambitions
Context
 : 
Our customers expect the same seamless user experience in shipping that the one they receive with packaging from companies like Amazon and AliExpress. This includes timely updates, event tracking, and accurate delivery predictions.
Must-have
 : Actual data (GPS and/or events at depot, terminal & customer premises) shared by 
haulier
Nice-to-have (2025): Estimated data, 
milages
, fuel type
